# MDVAL Cases(addition, rounding)
ieee_test_7000 = {
    set_temp_variable = { arg_a = 1260068.374 }
    set_temp_variable = { arg_b = 1260068.374 }

    set_temp_variable = { actual_output = 0 }
    ieeeAdd = yes

    set_temp_variable = { expected_output = 1268456.982 }

    set_temp_variable = { invalid = 0 }
    if = {
        limit = {
            OR = {
                NOT = { check_variable = { actual_output = expected_output } }
            }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { invalid = 1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = { invalid = 1 }
        }
        log = "Test [?test_id] - +MDVALA + +MDVALA - FAIL"
        add_to_temp_array = { test_fail_array = test_id }
    }
    else = {
        log = "Test [?test_id] - +MDVALA + +MDVALA - PASS"
    }

    set_temp_variable = { to_print_float = actual_output }
    log = "Actual: [print_float_full]"
    set_temp_variable = { to_print_float = expected_output }
    log = "Expected: [print_float_full]"
}

        add_to_temp_array = { test_fail_array = test_id }
    }
    else = {
        log = "Test [?test_id] - +POSNAN + +NEGINF - PASS"
    }

    set_temp_variable = { to_print_float = actual_output }
    log = "Actual: [print_float_full]"
    set_temp_variable = { to_print_float = expected_output }
    log = "Expected: [print_float_full]"
}
